# NI DOCUMENT BUNDLE: rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref

<!--NI_BUNDLE_CHUNK bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref start=1 end=200 -->
<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/configure-generation-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00001: Configure Generation

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/configure-generation-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/configure-generation-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure various parameters for the Bluetooth signal to generate using the toolkit. The help topics for some VIs do not contain parameter details. Refer to the corresponding property help topics for more information about these VIs. icon

### Configure Generation

Use the VIs on this palette to configure various parameters for the Bluetooth signal to generate using the toolkit.

Note

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='configure-generation-mnu.png']

- [niBT SG Property Node VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-sg-property-node-vi.html) Sets (writes) or gets (reads) niBT SG properties.
- [niBT SG Set Carrier Mode VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-carrier-mode-vi.html) Sets the Carrier Mode property.
- [niBT SG Set Oversampling Factor VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-oversampling-factor-vi.html) Sets the Oversampling Factor property.
- [niBT SG Set Auto Headroom Enabled VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-auto-headroom-enabled-vi.html) Sets the Auto Headroom Enabled property.
- [niBT SG Set Headroom VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-headroom-vi.html) Sets the Headroom property.
- [niBT SG Set Number of Idle Slots VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-number-of-idle-slots-vi.html) Sets the Number of Idle Slots property.
- [niBT SG Set Number of Unique Packets VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-number-of-unique-packets-vi.html) Sets the Number of Unique Packets property.
- [Configure Packet Settings](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/packet-control-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure the packet settings.
- [niBT SG Set Power Ramp Time VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-power-ramp-time-vi.html) Sets the Power Ramp Time property.
- [niBT SG Set Power Ramp Settling Time VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-power-ramp-settling-time-vi.html) Sets the Power Ramp Settling Time property.
- [Configure Impairments](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/impairments-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure impairments.

Parent topic:

Generation

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/data-mnu.html language=enus -->

### Configure User Payload

Use the VIs on this palette to configure the user payload.

Note

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='data-mnu.png']

- [niBT SG Set Payload Data Type VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-payload-data-type-vi.html) Sets the Payload Data Type property.
- [niBT SG Set Payload PN Order VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-payload-pn-order-vi.html) Sets the Payload PN Order property.
- [niBT SG Set Payload PN Seed VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-payload-pn-seed-vi.html) Sets the Payload PN Seed property.
- [niBT SG Set Payload User Defined Bits VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-payload-user-defined-bits-vi.html) Sets the Payload User Defined Bits property.

Parent topic:

Configure Packet Settings

## TOPIC 00003: Configure Dirty Tx Settings

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/dirty-tx-settings-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/dirty-tx-settings-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure dirty tx settings. The help topics for some VIs do not contain parameter details. Refer to the corresponding property help topics for more information about these VIs. icon

### Configure Dirty Tx Settings

Use the VIs on this palette to configure dirty tx settings.

Note

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='dirty-tx-settings-mnu.png']

- [niBT SG Set Dirty Tx Enabled VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-dirty-tx-enabled-vi.html) Sets the Dirty Tx Enabled property.
- [niBT SG Set Dirty Tx Mode VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-dirty-tx-mode-vi.html) Sets the Dirty Tx Mode property.
- [niBT SG Set Dirty Tx Parameter Set Enabled Set VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-dirty-tx-parameter-set-enabled-set-vi.html) Sets the Dirty Tx Parameters Enabled Set property.
- [niBT SG Set Dirty Tx Carrier Frequency Offset Set VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-dirty-tx-carrier-frequency-offset-set-vi.html) Sets the Dirty Tx Carrier Frequency Offset Set property.
- [niBT SG Set Dirty Tx Modulation Index Set VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-dirty-tx-modulation-index-set-vi.html) Sets the Dirty Tx Modulation Index Set property.
- [niBT SG Set Dirty Tx Symbol Timing Error Set VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-dirty-tx-symbol-timing-error-set-vi.html) Sets the Dirty Tx Symbol Timing Error Set property.
- [niBT SG Set Dirty Tx Residual FM Deviation VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-dirty-tx-residual-fm-deviation-vi.html) Sets the Dirty Tx Residual FM Deviation property.
- [niBT SG Set Dirty Tx Residual FM Frequency VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-dirty-tx-residual-fm-frequency-vi.html) Sets the Dirty Tx Residual FM Frequency property.
- [niBT SG Set Dirty Tx Modulation Index Type VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-dirty-tx-modulation-index-type-vi.html) Sets the Dirty Tx Modulation Index Type property.

Parent topic:

Configure Packet Settings

### Configure DV Voice Payload

Use the VIs on this palette to configure the data voice (DV) voice payload.

Note

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='dv-voice-mnu.png']

- [niBT SG Set DV Voice Payload Data Type VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/dv/nibt-sg-set-dv-voice-payload-data-type-vi.html) Sets the DV Voice Payload Data Type property.
- [niBT SG Set DV Voice Payload PN Order VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/dv/nibt-sg-set-dv-voice-payload-pn-order-vi.html) Sets the DV Voice Payload PN Order property.
- [niBT SG Set DV Voice Payload PN Seed VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/dv/nibt-sg-set-dv-voice-payload-pn-seed-vi.html) Sets the DV Voice Payload PN Seed property.

## TOPIC 00005: Configure FHS Payload

- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure the frequency-hopping synchronization (FHS) payload. The help topics for some VIs do not contain parameter details. Refer to the corresponding property help topics for more information about these VIs. icon

### Configure FHS Payload

Use the VIs on this palette to configure the frequency-hopping synchronization (FHS) payload.

Note

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='fhs-mnu.png']

- [niBT SG Set FHS Payload LT Address VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/fhs/nibt-sg-set-fhs-payload-lt-address-vi.html) Sets the FHS Payload LT Address property.
- [niBT SG Set FHS Payload Device Class VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/fhs/nibt-sg-set-fhs-payload-device-class-vi.html) Sets the FHS Payload Device Class property.
- [niBT SG Set FHS Payload Scan Repetition VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/fhs/nibt-sg-set-fhs-payload-scan-repetition-vi.html) Sets the FHS Payload Scan Repetition property.
- [niBT SG Set FHS Payload Page Scan Mode VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/fhs/nibt-sg-set-fhs-payload-page-scan-mode-vi.html) Sets the FHS Payload Page Scan Mode property.
- [niBT SG Set FHS Payload Device Clock VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/fhs/nibt-sg-set-fhs-payload-device-clock-vi.html) Sets the FHS Payload Device Clock property.
- [niBT SG Set FHS Payload BD Address VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/fhs/nibt-sg-set-fhs-payload-bd-address-vi.html) Sets the FHS Payload BD Address LAP , FHS Payload BD Address UAP , and FHS Payload BD Address NAP properties.

Parent topic:

Configure Packet Settings

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/file-io-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00006: File IO

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/file-io-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/file-io-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure the file input and output operations. The help topics for some VIs do not contain parameter details. Refer to the corresponding property help topics for more information about these VIs. icon

### File IO

Use the VIs on this palette to configure the file input and output operations.

Note

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='file-io-mnu.png']

- [niBT SG Save Configuration to File VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-sg-save-configuration-to-file-vi.html) Saves properties of the session, which you may have modified after opening the session, to a file located at the specified path.
- [niBT SG Create and Write Waveforms to File VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-sg-create-and-write-waveforms-to-file-vi.html) Creates waveforms according to the parameters you specify, and saves the waveforms to a file.
- [niBT SG Load Configuration from File VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-sg-load-configuration-from-file-vi.html) Reads values of session properties (configuration) saved in a file and sets these values to the corresponding properties on the session, thus restoring the state of the BT Generation to the original state when the file was saved.
- [niBT SG Read Waveform from File VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-sg-read-waveform-from-file-vi.html) Reads a waveform from a TDMS file. You can save this file using the Generation Interactive Example for Bluetooth . The niBT SG Read Waveform from File VI returns the I/Q complex waveform data that you can subsequently download to an RF signal generator device.

Parent topic:

Generation

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/generation-information-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00007: Generation Information

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/generation-information-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/generation-information-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to obtain generation information such as IQ rate, actual payload length, actual headroom, and toolkit compatibility version. The help topics for some VIs do not contain parameter details. Refer to the corresponding property help topics for more information about these VIs

### Generation Information

Use the VIs on this palette to obtain generation information such as IQ rate, actual payload length, actual headroom, and toolkit compatibility version.

Note

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='generation-information-mnu.png']

- [niBT SG Get IQ Rate VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-get-iq-rate-vi.html) Returns the IQ Rate property.
- [niBT SG Get Actual Payload Length VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-get-actual-payload-length-vi.html) Returns the Actual Payload Length property.
- [niBT SG Get Actual Headroom VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-get-actual-headroom-vi.html) Returns the Actual Headroom property.
- [niBT SG Get Toolkit Compatibility Version VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-get-toolkit-compatibility-version-vi.html) Returns the Toolkit Compatibility Version property.

Parent topic:

Generation

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/generation-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00008: Generation

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/generation-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/generation-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to set various parameters used for generating signals that confirm to the Bluetooth specifications, as well as for configuring NI RF vector signal generators for generating these signals. You can use the niBT SG Property Node to configure additional properties. © 2011–202

### Generation

Use the VIs on this palette to set various parameters used for generating signals that confirm to the Bluetooth specifications, as well as for configuring NI RF vector signal generators for generating these signals. You can use the [niBT SG Property Node](/csh?topicname=nibt-sg-property-node-vi.html) to configure additional properties.

© 2011–2026 National Instruments Corporation. All rights reserved.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='generation-mnu.png']

- [niBT SG Open Session VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-sg-open-session-vi.html) Looks up an existing niBT SG session using the session name parameter and returns the refnum that you can pass to subsequent niBT SG VIs and the niBT SG Property Node . If the look up fails, the niBT SG Open Session VI creates a new niBT SG session and returns a new refnum.
- [Configure Generation](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/configure-generation-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure various parameters for the Bluetooth signal to generate using the toolkit.
- [niBT SG Create Waveform (Complex Cluster) VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-sg-create-waveform-complex-cluster-vi.html) Creates a waveform according to the values that you specify. This VI generates one frame at a time.
- [niBT RFSG Create and Download Waveform VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-rfsg-create-and-download-waveform-vi.html) Creates the waveform according to the parameters that you specify, writes it into the NI RF vector signal generator memory, and stores the I/Q rate and headroom of the waveform in the RFSG database .
- [Generation Information](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/generation-information-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to obtain generation information such as IQ rate, actual payload length, actual headroom, and toolkit compatibility version.
- [RFSG Database](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/rfsg-database-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure, store, or retrieve information from the RFSG database.
- [niBT SG Channel Number to Carrier Frequency VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-sg-channel-number-to-carrier-frequency-vi.html) Computes the carrier frequency of the Bluetooth signal to generate based on the value that you specify in the channel number parameter. The BT Generation computes the center frequency according to section 2, Part A, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification Version v6.0 .
- [niBT SG Reset Session VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-sg-reset-session-vi.html) Resets all the properties of the session to their default values.
- [niBT SG Close Session VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/nibt-sg-close-session-vi.html) Closes the niBT SG session and releases resources associated with that session. Call this VI once for each unique named session that you have created.
- [File IO](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/file-io-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure the file input and output operations.

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/header-control-mnu.html language=enus -->

Note

## TOPIC 00011: Configure Impairments

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/impairments-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/impairments-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure impairments. The help topics for some VIs do not contain parameter details. Refer to the corresponding property help topics for more information about these VIs. icon

### Configure Impairments

Use the VIs on this palette to configure impairments.

Note

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='impairments-mnu.png']

- [niBT SG Set All IQ Impairments Enabled VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-all-iq-impairments-enabled-vi.html) Sets the All IQ Impairments Enabled property.
- [niBT SG Set IQ Gain Imbalance VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-iq-gain-imbalance-vi.html) Sets the IQ Gain Imbalance property.
- [niBT SG Set Quadrature Skew VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-quadrature-skew-vi.html) Sets the Quadrature Skew property.
- [niBT SG Set I DC Offset VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-i-dc-offset-vi.html) Sets the I DC Offset property.
- [niBT SG Set Q DC Offset VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-q-dc-offset-vi.html) Sets the Q DC Offset property.
- [niBT SG Set Carrier Frequency Offset VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-carrier-frequency-offset-vi.html) Sets the Carrier Frequency Offset property.
- [niBT SG Set AWGN Enabled VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-awgn-enabled-vi.html) Sets the AWGN Enabled property.
- [niBT SG Set Carrier to Noise Ratio VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-carrier-to-noise-ratio-vi.html) Sets the Carrier to Noise Ratio property.

Parent topic:

Configure Generation

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/packet-control-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00012: Configure Packet Settings

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/packet-control-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/packet-control-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure the packet settings. The help topics for some VIs do not contain parameter details. Refer to the corresponding property help topics for more information about these VIs. icon

### Configure Packet Settings

Use the VIs on this palette to configure the packet settings.

Note

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='packet-control-mnu.png']

- [niBT SG Set Packet Type VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-packet-type-vi.html) Sets the Packet Type property.
- [niBT SG Set Modulation Index VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-modulation-index-vi.html) Sets the Modulation Index property.
- [niBT SG Set BD Address VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-bd-address-vi.html) Sets the BD Address LAP , BD Address UAP , and BD Address NAP properties.
- [Configure Packet Header](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/header-control-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure the packet header.
- [Configure Payload Header](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/header-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure the payload header.
- [Configure User Payload](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/data-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure the user payload.
- [Configure FHS Payload](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/fhs-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure the frequency-hopping synchronization (FHS) payload.
- [Configure DV Voice Payload](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/dv-voice-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure the data voice (DV) voice payload.
- [niBT SG Set Whitening Enabled VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-whitening-enabled-vi.html) Sets the Whitening Enabled property.
- [niBT SG Set Whitening Clock VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-whitening-clock-vi.html) Sets the Whitening Clock property.
- [Configure Dirty Tx Settings](../../../../../menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/dirty-tx-settings-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure dirty tx settings.
- [niBT SG Set LE Access Address VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-le-access-address-vi.html) Sets the LE Access Address property.
- [niBT SG Set Antenna Relative Phase and Amplitude VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/sys/nibt-sg-set-antenna-relative-phase-and-amplitude-vi.html) Sets the Relative Phase and Relative Amplitude values for the non reference antennas An (1<n<=256) relative to the reference antenna A0, only when you set the Antenna Switching Enabled property True . The reference period and sampling slots in the constant tone extension (CTE) field are modulated in amplitude and phase as specified in the Antenna Switching Pattern property.

Parent topic:

Configure Generation

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/rfsg-database-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00013: RFSG Database

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/rfsg-database-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/rf-toolkits/bt/generation/rfsg-database-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure, store, or retrieve information from the RFSG database. icon

### RFSG Database

Use the VIs on this palette to configure, store, or retrieve information from the RFSG database.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfsg-database-mnu.png']

- [niBT RFSG Configure Script VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/rfsg-database/nibt-rfsg-configure-script-vi.html) Configures the I/Q rate and power level of the waveforms that you specify in the script parameter. This VI sets the niRFSG IQ Rate property to the I/Q rate in the RFSG database if the I/Q rates are the same for all the waveforms. The VI sets the niRFSG Power Level property to the sum of the power level that you specify in the power level parameter and the minimum headrooms of all the waveforms.
- [niBT RFSG Store IQ Rate VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/rfsg-database/nibt-rfsg-store-iq-rate-vi.html) Stores the I/Q rate, which you specify in the IQ rate parameter, in the RFSG database .
- [niBT RFSG Store Headroom VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/rfsg-database/nibt-rfsg-store-headroom-vi.html) Stores the headroom, which you specify in the headroom parameter, in the RFSG database .
- [niBT RFSG Retrieve IQ Rate (Script) VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/rfsg-database/nibt-rfsg-retrieve-iq-rate-script-vi.html) Checks the I/Q rate of all the waveforms in the script that you specify in the script parameter. This VI returns the I/Q rate if the I/Q rates are the same for all the waveforms. If the I/Q rates are different, the VI returns an error.
- [niBT RFSG Retrieve Minimum Headroom (Script) VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/rfsg-database/nibt-rfsg-retrieve-minimum-headroom-script-vi.html) Looks up the headroom of all the waveforms contained in the script and returns the minimum of all these headrooms, in dB.
- [niBT RFSG Retrieve IQ Rate (Waveform) VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/rfsg-database/nibt-rfsg-retrieve-iq-rate-waveform-vi.html) Returns the I/Q rate stored in the RFSG database . The VI uses the waveform name as the key to retrieve the waveform properties.
- [niBT RFSG Retrieve Headroom (Waveform) VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/rfsg-database/nibt-rfsg-retrieve-headroom-waveform-vi.html) Returns the headroom, in dB, stored in the RFSG database . The VI uses the waveform name as the key to retrieve the waveform properties.
- [niBT RFSG Clear Database VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rf-toolkits/bt/sg/rfsg-database/nibt-rfsg-clear-database-vi.html) Clears the properties stored in the RFSG database and clears the waveforms from the NI RF vector signal generator memory.

Parent topic:

Generation

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration-p.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00014: niBTGeneration Properties

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration-p.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration-p.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the niBT SG properties to access configuration options for Bluetooth applications. © 2011–2026 National Instruments Corporation. All rights reserved.

### niBTGeneration Properties

Use the niBT SG properties to access configuration options for Bluetooth applications.

© 2011–2026 National Instruments Corporation. All rights reserved.

- [Active Channel](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr74.html) Specifies the active channel string used to access all subsequent properties in a property node until a new active channel is specified.
- [Carrier Frequency (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr40.html) Specifies the carrier frequency. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [Carrier Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr1.html) Specifies whether the carrier is continuous or includes bursts.
- [Oversampling Factor](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr46.html) Specifies the number of times the Nyquist sample rate is increased to obtain the final sample rate of a signal.
- [Hardware Settings:Maximum Hardware IQ Rate (S/s)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr45.html) Specifies the maximum I/Q rate that the NI RF vector signal generator supports.
- [Hardware Settings:Auto Headroom Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr3.html) Specifies whether the BT Generation calculates the headroom or uses the value that you specify in the Headroom property.
- [Hardware Settings:Headroom (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr4.html) Specifies the value, in dB, for the headroom. The BT Generation uses this property for scaling the waveform when you set the Auto Headroom Enabled property to False .
- [Hardware Settings:Run Time Scaling (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr4f.html) Specifies the Runtime Scaling value in dB to store in the file along with the waveform.
- [Hardware Settings:Recommended Settings:IQ Rate (S/s)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr5.html) Returns the sample rate, in samples per second (S/s), for generation. The symbol rate of the Bluetooth signal is 1 megasymbol per second. The sample rate of the generated signal is the product of the symbol rate and the oversampling factor. The BT Generation uses an oversampling factor of 8.
- [Hardware Settings:Recommended Settings:Actual Headroom (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr6.html) Returns the actual headroom, in dB, used by the BT Generation. You can use this value to configure the peak power of the generation hardware.
- [Hardware Settings:Recommended Settings:Burst Start Locations []](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr5a.html) Returns an array of sample positions for the start of all bursts, within the waveform.
- [Hardware Settings:Recommended Settings:Burst Stop Locations []](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr5b.html) Returns an array of sample positions for the end of all bursts, within the waveform.
- [Packet Settings:Packet Type](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr7.html) Specifies the Bluetooth packet type.
- [Packet Settings:Modulation Index](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr44.html) Specifies the modulation index value for the Gaussian frequency shift keying modulation in Bluetooth packets.
- [Packet Settings:Bandwidth Bit Period Product](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr65.html) Specifies the bandwidth bit period product of GFSK modulation for LE-CS packet type.
- [Packet Settings:Data Rate (bps)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr66.html) Specifies the Higher Data Throughput (HDT) Bit Rate. This value is expressed in bps. This property is applicable only when you set the packet type to LE-HDT.
- [Packet Settings:BD Address:LAP](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr8.html) Specifies the 24-bit lower address part (LAP) of the Bluetooth device address.
- [Packet Settings:BD Address:UAP](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr9.html) Specifies the 8-bit upper address part (UAP) of the Bluetooth device address.
- [Packet Settings:BD Address:NAP](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attra.html) Specifies the 16-bit non-significant address part (NAP) of the Bluetooth device address.
- [Packet Settings:Packet Header:LT Address](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attrb.html) Specifies the 3-bit logical transport (LT) address of the packet. The LT address field indicates the destination slave for a packet in a master-to-slave transmission slot and indicates the source slave for a slave-to-master transmission slot. Refer to sections 6.4.1 and 6.4.2, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the LT address of a packet.
- [Packet Settings:Packet Header:FLOW](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attrc.html) Specifies the value for the flow control field in the packet header. This field controls the 1-bit flow control parameter in the packet. Refer to Section 6.4.3, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the flow control field.
- [Packet Settings:Packet Header:ARQN](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attrd.html) Specifies the value for the automatic repeat request number (ARQN) field in the packet header. This property controls the value for the 1-bit acknowledgement indicator, which indicates whether the data packet transfer is successful. Refer to sections 6.4.4 and 7.6, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the ARQN field.
- [Packet Settings:Packet Header:SEQN](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attre.html) Specifies the value for the sequential numbering scheme (SEQN) field in the packet header. This property controls the value for the 1-bit sequence bit, which allows you to provide a sequential numbering scheme to order the data packet scheme. Refer to sections 6.4.5, 7.6.2, and 7.6.5, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the SEQN field.
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:Header Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr42.html) Specifies whether to enable the payload header in the Bluetooth packet to be generated. This is applicable only for LE packets.
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:LLID](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attrf.html) Specifies whether the payload is the start or continuation fragment of a logical link control and adaptation protocol (L2CAP) or link management protocol (LMP) message.
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:FLOW](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr10.html) Specifies the value for the flow control bit in the payload header. This field controls the 1-bit flow control parameter in the packet.
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:Length Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr2b.html) Specifies whether the BT Generation automatically sets the value of the LENGTH field in the payload header to the maximum permissible length or whether it uses the value that you specify in the Payload Length property.
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:Length (bytes)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr11.html) Specifies the payload length, in bytes. If the length exceeds the maximum permissible length mentioned in the Bluetooth specification, the BT Generation uses this maximum permissible length as the payload length. For LE-TP-EXT and LE-Enhanced packet types, typical LE packet is generated length up to 255 bytes, and Hyper Length LE packet is generated for length from 256 bytes to 8191 bytes. For LE HDT packet, Format0 supports payload length up to 510 bytes, whereas Format1 supports up to 8191 bytes per payload. In the case of LE HDT Format1, when the Payload Zone Configuration Mode is set to Auto and the Payload Length Mode is set to User Defined, you must specify 'payload x' as the active channel string to configure this property.
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:Number of Payloads](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr6d.html) Specifies the number of payloads for the LE-HDT packet when HDT Packet Format is set to Format1 . The valid values are 1 to 4.
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:Format1 Payload Zone Configuration Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr6e.html) Specifies the payload zone configuration mode for the LE-HDT packet when HDT Packet Format is set to Format1 .
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:TxLen Sequence Number](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr6f.html) Specifies the value of TxLen SN field of Tx Portion of PDU Header. This property is valid only for the LE-HDT packet when HDT Packet Format is set to Format1 and Format1 Payload Zone Configuration Mode is set to User Defined .
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:Number of Blocks](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr70.html) Specifies the number of blocks minus one that the payload is split into. This property is valid only for the LE-HDT packet when HDT Packet Format is set to Format1 and Format1 Payload Zone Configuration Mode is set to User Defined .
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:Block Size (bytes)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr71.html) Specifies the block size of each block specified by Number of Blocks . This property is valid only for the LE-HDT packet when HDT Packet Format is set to Format1 and Format1 Payload Zone Configuration Mode is set to User Defined .
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:Last Block Size (bytes)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr72.html) Specifies the block size of the last block. The valid values are 1 to 8191 Bytes.
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:TxBlock Map](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr73.html) Specifies the TxBlockMap field of Tx Portion of PDU Header. The TxBlockMap field is 8 or 16 bits depending on the value of TxLen Sequence Number . It indicates which blocks are actually being transmitted in the packet, with bit b set to 1 if block b (counting from 0) is included and 0 if it is not. At least one bit shall be set.
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:Actual Length (bytes)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr2c.html) Returns the actual payload length, in bytes.
- [Packet Settings:Payload Header:Payload Zone Length (bytes)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr75.html) Returns the payload zone length of LE-HDT packets. The payload zone length has all payloads and each payload contains blocks followed by CRCs.
- [Packet Settings:User Payload:Data Type](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr12.html) Specifies the type of payload data for the packet.
- [Packet Settings:User Payload:PN Order](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr29.html) Specifies the order (length of memory) of the pseudorandom bit sequence (PRBS) generator. If you set the Payload Data Type property to User Defined Bits , the BT Generation ignores the Payload PN Order property.
- [Packet Settings:User Payload:PN Seed](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr2a.html) Specifies the initialization seed used for the pseudorandom bit sequence (PRBS) generator. If you set the Data Type property to User Defined Bits , the BT Generation ignores the Payload PN Seed property.
- [Packet Settings:User Payload:User Defined Bits []](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr14.html) Specifies a bit pattern as an array of zeros and ones.
- [Packet Settings:FHS Payload:LT Address](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr15.html) Specifies the 3-bit logical transport (LT) address of the frequency hop synchronization (FHS) packet. Refer to Section 6.5.1.4, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the LT address of the FHS packet.
- [Packet Settings:FHS Payload:Device Class](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr16.html) Specifies the 24-bit field in the frequency hop synchronization (FHS) packet payload. This field indicates the class of device of the device that sends the FHS packet. Refer to Section 6.5.1.4, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the device class field in the FHS packet payload.
- [Packet Settings:FHS Payload:Scan Repetition](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr18.html) Specifies the 2-bit field in the frequency hop synchronization (FHS) packet payload. This field indicates the interval between two consecutive page scan windows. Refer to Section 6.5.1.4, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the payload scan repetition field of the FHS packet payload.
- [Packet Settings:FHS Payload:Page Scan Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr19.html) Specifies the 3-bit field in the frequency hop synchronization (FHS) packet payload. This field indicates the default scan mode used by the sender of the FHS packet. Refer to Section 6.5.1.4, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the page scan mode field of the FHS packet payload.
- [Packet Settings:FHS Payload:Device Clock](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr1a.html) Specifies the 26-bit field in the frequency hop synchronization (FHS) packet payload. This field contains the value of the native clock of the device that sends the FHS packet. Refer to Section 6.5.1.4, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the device clock field of the FHS packet payload.
- [Packet Settings:FHS Payload:BD Address:LAP](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr1b.html) Specifies the 24-bit field in the frequency hop synchronization (FHS) packet payload. This field contains the lower address part (LAP) of the device that sends the FHS packet.
- [Packet Settings:FHS Payload:BD Address:UAP](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr1c.html) Specifies the 8-bit field in the frequency hop synchronization (FHS) packet payload. This field contains the upper address part (UAP) of the device that sends the FHS packet.
- [Packet Settings:FHS Payload:BD Address:NAP](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr1d.html) Specifies the 16-bit field in the frequency hop synchronization (FHS) packet payload. This field contains the nonsignificant address part (NAP) of the device that sends the FHS packet. Refer to Section 6.5.1.4, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the NAP field.
- [Packet Settings:DV Voice Payload:Data Type](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr31.html) Specifies the type of payload data for the data voice (DV) packet.
- [Packet Settings:DV Voice Payload:PN Order](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr2e.html) Specifies the order (length of memory) of the pseudorandom bit sequence (PRBS) generator. If you set the DV Voice Payload Data Type property to User Defined Bits , the BT Generation ignores the DV Voice Payload PN Order property.
- [Packet Settings:DV Voice Payload:PN Seed](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr2f.html) Specifies the initialization seed used for the pseudorandom bit sequence (PRBS) generator. If you set the Data Type property to DV Voice Payload User Defined Bits , the BT Generation ignores the DV Voice Payload PN Seed property.
- [Packet Settings:DV Voice Payload:User Defined Bits []](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr30.html) Specifies a bit pattern as an array of zeros and ones.
- [Packet Settings:LE-TP Payload:Payload Type](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr32.html) Specifies the type of payload used for the LE and LE CS packets.
- [Packet Settings:LE-TP Payload:Corrupt Alternate CRC](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr36.html) Specifies whether the BT Generation intentionally corrupts the cyclic redundancy check (CRC) portion of every alternate packet generated. Refer to Section 6.3.7 of the Bluetooth Test Specification RFPHY.TS.p22 . CRC corruption is done by toggling the seed used for CRC computation.
- [Packet Settings:Direction Finding:Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr4b.html) Specifies the mode for direction finding. The property is valid only for LE-TP, LE-TP EXT, LE-Enhanced and LE-HDT packet type.
- [Packet Settings:Direction Finding:Constant Tone Extension Length (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr4d.html) Specifies the length of the constant tone extension field in the generated signal. This value is expressed in seconds. This property is applicable only when you set the Direction Finding Mode to either Angle of Arrival or Angle of Departure .
- [Packet Settings:Direction Finding:Constant Tone Extension Slot Duration](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr4e.html) Specifies the length of the antenna switching and sampling slots in the constant tone extension field. This value is expressed in seconds.
- [Packet Settings:Direction Finding:Antenna Switching Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr56.html) Specifies whether antenna switching is enabled for the generated low energy (LE) packets. This property is applicable only when you set the Direction Finding Mode to either Angle of Arrival or Angle of Departure .
- [Packet Settings:Direction Finding:Number of Antennas](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr52.html) Specifies the number of antennas used to transmit or receive the constant tone extension (CTE) portion of low energy (LE) packet. This property is applicable only when you set the Antenna Switching Enabled property to True .
- [Packet Settings:Direction Finding:Antenna Switching Pattern](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr55.html) Specifies the pattern in which the antennas switch in constant tone extension (CTE) portion of the low energy (LE) packet. The current definition always treats A0 as the reference antenna. A1, A2, A3...Am are all non-reference antennas. This property is applicable only when you set the Antenna Switching Enabled to True .
- [Packet Settings:Direction Finding:Antenna Switching Duration (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr57.html) Specifies the duration for which the transitions of phase and amplitude take place in the switching slots of the constant tone extension (CTE) portion of the low energy (LE) packet. This property is applicable only when you set the Antenna Switching Enabled property to True .
- [Packet Settings:Direction Finding:Antenna Switching Duration Used (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr58.html) Returns the actual duration used to make the transitions of phase and amplitude in the switching slots of the constant tone extension (CTE) portion of low energy (LE) packet. This property is applicable only when you set the Antenna Switching Enabled property to True .
- [Packet Settings:Channel Sounding:Packet Format](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr5c.html) Specifies the channel sounding (CS) packet format. This property is applicable only when you set the packet type to either LE-CS-1M or LE-CS-2M .
- [Packet Settings:Channel Sounding:SYNC Sequence](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr5d.html) Specifies whether the sounding sequence field is present in SYNC packet. This property is applicable for all CS Packet formats except CS Tone.
- [Packet Settings:Channel Sounding:Phase Measurement Period](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr5e.html) Specifies the phase measurement period in the generated CS packet. This property is applicable for all CS packet formats except SYNC.
- [Packet Settings:Channel Sounding:Sequence Length (bits)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr5f.html) Specifies sounding sequence length, in bits. This property is applicable only when you set the CS SYNC Sequence to Sounding Sequence.
- [Packet Settings:Channel Sounding:Sequence Marker Signals []](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr60.html) Specifies an array of sounding sequence marker signals. This property is applicable only when you set the CS SYNC Sequence to Sounding Sequence.
- [Packet Settings:Channel Sounding:Sequence Marker Positions []](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr61.html) Specifies an array of sounding sequence marker positions at which sounding sequence marker signals are inserted. This property is applicable only when you set the CS SYNC Sequence to Sounding Sequence.
- [Packet Settings:Channel Sounding:Tone Extension Slot Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr62.html) Specifies whether CS tone extension slot is present in generated LE CS packets. This property is applicable for all CS packet formats except SYNC.
- [Packet Settings:High Data Throughput:Zadoff-Chu Index](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr69.html) Specifies Zadoff-Chu Index for the Long Training Sequence in the preamble.
- [Packet Settings:High Data Throughput:Physical Channel Address](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr6a.html) Specifies the 40-bit physical channel address of Higher Data Throughput (HDT) packet.
- [Packet Settings:High Data Throughput:Packet Format](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr67.html) Specifies the Higher Data Throughput (HDT) packet format. This property is applicable only for LE HDT packet type
- [Packet Settings:High Data Throughput:Payload CRC Seed](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr76.html) Specifies the 32 bit CRC initialization seed value. This property is applicable only when user set the Packet Type to LE-HDT and HDT Packet Format is set to Format0 or Format1 .
- [Packet Settings:High Data Throughput:PHY Interval (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr68.html) Specifies the physical layer intervals. This property is valid only for Format1 packet format. This value is expressed in seconds.
- [Packet Settings:High Data Throughput:VHDT Mode Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr6b.html)
- [Packet Settings:High Data Throughput:Number of Block Repetition Sequences](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr6c.html)
- [Packet Settings:Whitening Settings:Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr1f.html) Specifies whether to enable the whitening settings.
- [Packet Settings:Whitening Settings:Clock](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr20.html) Specifies the 28-bit master Bluetooth device clock. This property is applicable only to BR and EDR packets. The BT Generation uses this property to initialize the linear feedback shift register used for calculating the whitening word. The BT Generation uses bits 1 to 6 for this purpose. Refer to sections 1.1 and 7.2, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the Bluetooth device clock.
- [Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr1e.html) Specifies whether to enable the dirty transmitter .
- [Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr37.html) Specifies whether to enable the dirty transmitter with the standard settings, the user-defined settings or the frequency drift.
- [Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Modulation Index Type](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr43.html) Specifies whether the modulation index type is Standard or Stable .
- [Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Parameters Enabled Set []](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr38.html) Specifies the number of impairment sets you must enable out of the ten sets in LE and BR or the three sets in EDR. This property is applicable if you set the Dirty Tx Mode property to User Defined . The BT Generation ignores this property if you set the Dirty Tx Mode property to Standard .
- [Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Carrier Frequency Offset Set []](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr39.html) Specifies the offset value of each of the impairment set that you enable in the Dirty Tx Parameters Enabled Set property.
- [Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Modulation Index Set []](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr3a.html) Specifies the modulation index value of each of the impairment set that you enable in the Dirty Tx Parameters Enabled Set property.
- [Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Symbol Timing Error Set []](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr3b.html) Specifies the symbol timing error value of each of the impairment set that you enable in the Dirty Tx Parameters Enabled Set [] property.
- [Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Residual FM Deviation (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr3e.html) Specifies the frequency deviation of the modulated signal to provide the additional frequency drift. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Residual FM Frequency (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr3f.html) Specifies the frequency of the modulated signal to provide the additional frequency drift. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [Packet Settings:LE Access Address](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr3d.html) Specifies the 32-bit LE access address.
- [Packet Settings:Number of Unique Packets](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr33.html) Specifies the number of unique packets for which the pseudonoise (PN) generator must run continuously. The BT Generation resets the PN generator after it generates the number of packets that you specify in this property. For example, if you set this property to 1, the same payload is used in every packet; and if you set this property to 2, the same payload is used after every 2 packets. Configure this property only if you set the Payload Data Type property to PN Sequence .
- [Packet Settings:Number of Idle Slots](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr34.html) Specifies the number of idle slots that the BT Generation appends at the end of each valid packet.
- [Packet Settings:Packet Bit Sequence Trace Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr49.html) Specifies whether to enable the packet bit sequence trace.
- [Power Ramp Settings:Ramp Time (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr48.html) Specifies the ramp time of the burst. The ramp time is the time interval from the time when output power is 40 dB less than the final output power (X dBm) to the time when the output power is +/- 3 dB of the final output power. This value is expressed in seconds. The active packet duration for LE-TP packet is 376 microseconds.
- [Power Ramp Settings:Settling Time (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr47.html) Specifies the settling time of the burst. The settling time is the time interval from the time when output power is 40 dB less than the final output power (X dBm) to the time when the output power is +/- 1 dB of the final output power. This value is expressed in seconds. The active packet duration for LE-TP packet is 376 microseconds.
- [Impairments:IQ Impairments:Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr17.html) Specifies whether to enable I/Q impairments.
- [Impairments:IQ Impairments:IQ Gain Imbalance (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr21.html) Specifies the ratio, in dB, of the mean amplitude of the in-phase (I) signal to the mean amplitude of the quadrature-phase (Q) signal.
- [Impairments:IQ Impairments:Quadrature Skew (deg)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr22.html) Specifies the deviation in angle from 90 degrees between the in-phase (I) and quadrature-phase (Q) signals.
- [Impairments:IQ Impairments:I DC Offset (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr23.html) Specifies the value of the DC offset in the in-phase (I) signal as a percentage of the peak magnitude of the complex I/Q signal.
- [Impairments:IQ Impairments:Q DC Offset (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr24.html) Specifies the value of the DC offset in the quadrature-phase (Q) signal as percentage of the peak magnitude of the complex I/Q signal.
- [Impairments:Carrier Frequency Offset (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr25.html) Specifies the carrier frequency offset from the value that you specify as the center frequency of the RF signal generator. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [Impairments:Sample Clock Offset (ppm)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr63.html) Specifies the offset in the Sample Clock frequency from the sample frequency for CS packets. This value is expressed in parts per million (ppm).
- [Impairments:Time Delay (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr64.html) Specifies the time delay for CS packets. This value is expressed in seconds.
- [Impairments:AWGN:AWGN Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr26.html) Specifies whether to add additive white Gaussian noise (AWGN) to the baseband waveform.
- [Impairments:AWGN:Carrier to Noise Ratio (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr27.html) Specifies the carrier-to-noise ratio (CNR), in dB, of the waveform generated. Noise bandwidth is equal to half the value of the IQ Rate property. Configure the Carrier to Noise Ratio property only if you set the AWGN Enabled property to True .
- [Advanced:Waveform Size](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr2d.html) Returns the size, in complex samples, for a packet as specified by the Packet Type property and the number of idle slots specified by the Number of Idle Slots property.
- [Advanced:Waveform File Version](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr51.html) Specifies the waveform file version to be saved.
- [Advanced:Toolkit Compatibility Version](../../../resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr28.html) Indicates the toolkit compatibility version parameter of the niBT SG Open Session VI.

## TOPIC 00015: Carrier Mode

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr1.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr1.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether the carrier is continuous or includes bursts. If you set this property to Burst, the BT Generation generates the burst signal by adding zeros at the end of the packet to create one or more complete slots, depending on the packet type. In this mode, the BT Generation also shapes the

### Carrier Mode

Specifies whether the carrier is continuous or includes bursts.

If you set this property to **Burst**, the BT Generation generates the burst signal by adding zeros at the end of the packet to create one or more complete slots, depending on the packet type. In this mode, the BT Generation also shapes the generated waveform to meet the burst ramp characteristics specified in the *Bluetooth Test Purposes (TP) specification 1.2/2.0+EDR/2.1/2.1+EDR/3.0/3.0+HS*. If you set this property to **Continuous**, the BT Generation generates a phase continuous Bluetooth signal, which is used as an interference signal. This mode is useful to generate an interference signal with pseudorandom bits and continuous phase. In this mode, the Number of Idle Slots property is not used, and the number of idle slots is assumed be zero. In this mode, NI recommends you to leave the Number of Unique Packets, Payload Data Type, and Dirty Tx Enabled properties at their default values.

The following figure shows the envelope when you set the Carrier Mode property to **Burst**, and the [Packet Type](attr7.html) property is set to **DH1**.

[IMAGE alt='image' src='carriermode1.gif']

The following figure shows the envelope when you set the Carrier Mode property to **Continuous**.

[IMAGE alt='image' src='carriermode2.gif']

The default value is **Burst**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Carrier Mode |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | niBT SG Set Carrier Mode |
| Resettable | Yes |

| Burst | 0 | Specifies that the carrier mode includes bursts. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Continuous | 1 | Specifies that the carrier mode is continuous. |

Parent topic:

niBTGeneration Properties

### Packet Settings:Payload Header:FLOW

Specifies the value for the flow control bit in the payload header. This field controls the 1-bit flow control parameter in the packet.

The default value is 0. Valid values are 0, which indicates a Stop condition, and 1, which indicates a Go condition.

## TOPIC 00017: Packet Settings:Payload Header:Length (bytes)

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr11.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr11.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the payload length, in bytes. If the length exceeds the maximum permissible length mentioned in the Bluetooth specification, the BT Generation uses this maximum permissible length as the payload length. For LE-TP-EXT and LE-Enhanced packet types, typical LE packet is generated length up to

### Packet Settings:Payload Header:Length (bytes)

Specifies the payload length, in bytes. If the length exceeds the maximum permissible length mentioned in the Bluetooth specification, the BT Generation uses this maximum permissible length as the payload length. For LE-TP-EXT and LE-Enhanced packet types, typical LE packet is generated length up to 255 bytes, and Hyper Length LE packet is generated for length from 256 bytes to 8191 bytes. For LE HDT packet, Format0 supports payload length up to 510 bytes, whereas Format1 supports up to 8191 bytes per payload. In the case of LE HDT Format1, when the Payload Zone Configuration Mode is set to Auto and the Payload Length Mode is set to User Defined, you must specify 'payload x' as the active channel string to configure this property.

The default value is 0.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Payload Length (bytes) |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | niBT SG Set Payload Length |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

niBTGeneration Properties

## TOPIC 00019: Packet Settings:User Payload:User Defined Bits []

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr14.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr14.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies a bit pattern as an array of zeros and ones. If the array length is greater than the required payload length, the BT Generation uses a subset of the required length from the beginning of the array for waveform generation. If the array length is less than the required payload length, the BT

### Packet Settings:User Payload:User Defined Bits []

Specifies a bit pattern as an array of zeros and ones.

If the array length is greater than the required payload length, the BT Generation uses a subset of the required length from the beginning of the array for waveform generation. If the array length is less than the required payload length, the BT Generation repeats the bit pattern until the required length is achieved. If you set the [Data Type](attr12.html) property to **PN Sequence**, the BT Generation ignores the User Defined Bits property.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Payload User Defined Bits |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | niBT SG Set Payload User Defined Bits |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

niBTGeneration Properties

### Packet Settings:FHS Payload:Scan Repetition

## TOPIC 00024: Packet Settings:FHS Payload:Page Scan Mode

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr19.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr19.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the 3-bit field in the frequency hop synchronization (FHS) packet payload. This field indicates the default scan mode used by the sender of the FHS packet. Refer to Section 6.5.1.4, Part B, Volume 2 of the Bluetooth Specification v6.0 for more information about the page scan mode field of

### Packet Settings:FHS Payload:Page Scan Mode

Specifies the 3-bit field in the frequency hop synchronization (FHS) packet payload. This field indicates the default scan mode used by the sender of the FHS packet. Refer to Section 6.5.1.4, Part B, Volume 2 of the *Bluetooth Specification v6.0* for more information about the page scan mode field of the FHS packet payload.

The default value is 0. Valid values are 0 to 7, inclusive.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | FHS Payload Page Scan Mode |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | niBT SG Set FHS Payload Page Scan Mode |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

Remarks The following table lists the characteristics of this property. Short Na

### Packet Settings:Whitening Settings:Enabled

Specifies whether to enable the whitening settings.

If you set this property to **True** and the [Packet Type](attr7.html) property to any LE packets, you should set a value for the [Carrier Frequency](attr40.html) property.

The default value is **False**.

| --- | --- |

| High-level VIs | niBT SG Set Whitening Enabled |
| Resettable | Yes |

| False | 0 | Disables whitening. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| True | 1 | Enables whitening. |

## TOPIC 00031: Packet Settings:Whitening Settings:Clock

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr20.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr20.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the 28-bit master Bluetooth device clock. This property is applicable only to BR and EDR packets. The BT Generation uses this property to initialize the linear feedback shift register used for calculating the whitening word. The BT Generation uses bits 1 to 6 for this purpose. Refer to sec

### Packet Settings:Whitening Settings:Clock

Specifies the 28-bit master Bluetooth device clock. This property is applicable only to BR and EDR packets. The BT Generation uses this property to initialize the linear feedback shift register used for calculating the whitening word. The BT Generation uses bits 1 to 6 for this purpose. Refer to sections 1.1 and 7.2, Part B, Volume 2 of the *Bluetooth Specification v6.0* for more information about the Bluetooth device clock.

The default value is 0.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Whitening Clock |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | niBT SG Set Whitening Clock |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

niBTGeneration Properties

[IMAGE alt='image' src='IQgainimbalance5.gif']

### Impairments:AWGN:Carrier to Noise Ratio (dB)

Specifies the carrier-to-noise ratio (CNR), in dB, of the waveform generated. Noise bandwidth is equal to half the value of the [IQ Rate](/csh?topicname=attr5.html) property. Configure the Carrier to Noise Ratio property only if you set the [AWGN Enabled](/csh?topicname=attr26.html) property to **True**.

The default value is 50.

| Resettable | Yes |

## TOPIC 00043: Packet Settings:Payload Header:Actual Length (bytes)

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr2c.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr2c.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Returns the actual payload length, in bytes. If you set the Payload Length Mode property to Maximum Length, the BT Generation returns the maximum permissible payload data length as specified in the Bluetooth specifications. If you set the Payload Length Mode property to User Defined, the BT Generati

### Packet Settings:Payload Header:Actual Length (bytes)

Returns the actual payload length, in bytes.

If you set the [Payload Length Mode](attr2b.html) property to **Maximum Length**, the BT Generation returns the maximum permissible payload data length as specified in the Bluetooth specifications. If you set the Payload Length Mode property to **User Defined**, the BT Generation returns the value that you specify in the [Payload Length](attr11.html) property. If the value that you specify in the Payload Length property exceeds the maximum permissible payload length for the packet, the BT Generation returns this maximum permissible payload length.

For LE-HDT Packet type when [HDT Packet Format](attr67.html) is set to **Format1** and [Format1 Payload Zone Configuration Mode](attr6e.html) is set to **User Defined**, the Actual Payload Length is computed as Payload length = (Nb * [Block Size](attr71.html) ) + [Last Block Size](attr72.html) for each payload. Here Nb is number of transmitted blocks, depends on the [TxBlock Map](attr73.html) property.

You must use "payload x" as the active channel string to configure this property for LE-HDT Packet type when [HDT Packet Format](attr67.html) is set to **Format1**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Actual Payload Length (bytes) |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read Only |
| High-level VIs | niBT SG Get Actual Payload Length |
| Resettable | No |

Parent topic:

niBTGeneration Properties

### Hardware Settings:Auto Headroom Enabled

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | niBT SG Set Auto Headroom Enabled |
| Resettable | Yes |

| False | 0 | Specifies that the BT Generation uses the headroom that you specify in the Headroom property. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| True | 1 | Specifies that the BT Generation computes the headroom value based on the peak power of the signal. The BT Generation assumes that the generated signal average power is 0 dB. The BT Generation adds a power margin of 1.5 dB to the peak power to give some room for the filters in the NI RF vector signal generator. You can read the value of the computed headroom using the Actual Headroom property. |

## TOPIC 00048: Packet Settings:DV Voice Payload:User Defined Bits []

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr30.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr30.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies a bit pattern as an array of zeros and ones. If the array length is greater than the required payload length, the BT Generation uses a subset of the required length from the beginning of the array for waveform generation. If the array length is less than the required payload length, the BT

### Packet Settings:DV Voice Payload:User Defined Bits []

Specifies a bit pattern as an array of zeros and ones.

If the array length is greater than the required payload length, the BT Generation uses a subset of the required length from the beginning of the array for waveform generation. If the array length is less than the required payload length, the BT Generation repeats the bit pattern until the required length is achieved. If you set the [DV Voice Payload Data Type](attr31.html) property to **PN Sequence**, the BT Generation ignores the DV Voice Payload User Defined Bits property.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | DV Voice Payload User Defined Bits |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | niBT SG Set DV Voice Payload User Defined Bits |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

niBTGeneration Properties

## TOPIC 00051: Packet Settings:Number of Unique Packets

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr33.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr33.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the number of unique packets for which the pseudonoise (PN) generator must run continuously. The BT Generation resets the PN generator after it generates the number of packets that you specify in this property. For example, if you set this property to 1, the same payload is used in every p

### Packet Settings:Number of Unique Packets

Specifies the number of unique packets for which the pseudonoise (PN) generator must run continuously. The BT Generation resets the PN generator after it generates the number of packets that you specify in this property. For example, if you set this property to 1, the same payload is used in every packet; and if you set this property to 2, the same payload is used after every 2 packets. Configure this property only if you set the [Payload Data Type](/csh?topicname=attr12.html) property to **PN Sequence**.

For the bit error rate (BER) loop in device under test (DUT) measurements, set this property to the same value as the [BER Number of Unique Packets](/csh?context=rfmxbtgen_lvbtanalysisprop_attr1e) property. For PER loop through measurements with a DUT, set this property to the same value as the [PER Number of Packets](/csh?context=rfmxbtgen_lvbtanalysisprop_attr124) property.

Refer to the [Dirty Transmitter](/csh?context=rfmxbtgen_btgen_dirty_tx) topic for more information about the restrictions on the value of the Number of Unique Packets property.

The default value is 1.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Number of Unique Packets |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | niBT SG Set Number of Unique Packets |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

niBTGeneration Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr34.html language=enus -->

## TOPIC 00053: Packet Settings:LE-TP Payload:Corrupt Alternate CRC

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr36.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr36.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether the BT Generation intentionally corrupts the cyclic redundancy check (CRC) portion of every alternate packet generated. Refer to Section 6.3.7 of the Bluetooth Test Specification RFPHY.TS.p22. CRC corruption is done by toggling the seed used for CRC computation. The default value i

### Packet Settings:LE-TP Payload:Corrupt Alternate CRC

Specifies whether the BT Generation intentionally corrupts the cyclic redundancy check (CRC) portion of every alternate packet generated. Refer to Section 6.3.7 of the *Bluetooth Test Specification RFPHY.TS.p22*. CRC corruption is done by toggling the seed used for CRC computation.

The default value is **False**.

Note

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | LE-TP Corrupt Alternate CRC |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

| False | 0 | Disables CRC corruption of alternate LE packets. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| True | 1 | Enables CRC corruption of alternate LE packets. Set the Number of Unique Packets property to an even number when you set the LE-TP Corrupt Alternate CRC property to True. |

### Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Mode

### Packet Settings:Dirty Tx Settings:Modulation Index Set []

Specifies the modulation index value of each of the impairment set that you enable in the [Dirty Tx Parameters Enabled Set](/csh?topicname=attr38.html) property.

This property is applicable when you set the [Dirty Tx Mode](attr37.html) property to **User Defined**. The BT Generation ignores this property if you set the [Dirty Tx Mode](attr37.html) property to **Standard**.

Valid values are 0.28 to 0.4 for Basic Rate and EDR packets and 0.45 to 0.55 for LE packets, inclusive. The valid values are 0.495 to 0.505, inclusive, for LE packets when you set the [Dirty Tx Modulation Index Type](attr43.html) property to **Stable**.

## TOPIC 00059: Packet Settings:LE Access Address

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr3d.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr3d.html
- document_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the 32-bit LE access address. The Bluetooth core specification recommends to use 0x71764129 as the LE access address for all test packets. The preamble of LE-TP/LE-TP-EXT packets is either 01010101b or 10101010b, depending on the LSB of the LE access address. If the LSB of the LE access ad

### Packet Settings:LE Access Address

Specifies the 32-bit LE access address.

The Bluetooth core specification recommends to use 0x71764129 as the LE access address for all test packets. 
The preamble of LE-TP/LE-TP-EXT packets is either 01010101b or 10101010b, depending on the LSB of the LE access address. 
If the LSB of the LE access address is 1, the preamble shall be 01010101b, otherwise the preamble shall be 10101010b. This will be 0101010101010101b, 1010101010101010b respectively for LE-Enhanced packets.

The default value is 0x71764129.

Note

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | LE Access Address |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| High-level VIs | N/A |
| Resettable | Yes |

Parent topic:

niBTGeneration Properties

## TOPIC 00064: Packet Settings:Payload Header:Header Enabled

- bundle_id: `rfmxbtgen-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/nibtgeneration-rc/nibtgeneration/attr42.html`
